üìú PATH-PULSE: THE EXPLORER‚ÄôS OATH
Subject: System Access & Biological Data Protocols

Status: REQUIRED FOR INITIALIZATION

By tapping "INITIALIZE SYSTEM," you (hereafter referred to as "The Explorer") agree to the following protocols and terms of service:

1. The Bio-Data Protocol (Privacy)
The Path-Pulse Lab takes data integrity seriously.

Data Collection: You authorize the Lab to sync with your device‚Äôs health sensors (GPS, Heart Rate, Biometrics).

Encryption: Your biological data is encrypted and used solely for generating your Diagnostic Reports and Metabolic Fueling plans.

Social Sharing: You acknowledge that any Tactical Time-Lapses or Mission Briefings you share to social networks are at your own discretion. Once shared, they are visible to the "Global Grid."

2. Kinetic Liability (Safety)
Exploration involves real-world variables.

Situational Awareness: The Explorer must maintain 100% awareness of their physical surroundings. Do not stare at the Tactical Overlay while crossing intersections or traversing hazardous terrain.

Physical Limits: The "Expeditions" and "Protocols" generated by the Lab are suggestions based on data. If your physical "hardware" (your body) signals pain or exhaustion, you must override the app and cease activity. Path-Pulse is not liable for over-exertion or environmental hazards.

3. The Fueling & Nutrition Directive
Not Medical Advice: The Metabolic Fueling and Meal Prep suggestions are based on general nutritional science and your logged data. They do not replace the advice of a medical professional or nutritionist.

Accuracy: Calorie counting is an estimate. The Lab is only as accurate as the data you input.

4. Code of the Global Grid (Conduct)
Fair Play: Explorers shall not use external vehicles (cars, bikes, drones) to "spoof" GPS data for rank progression.

Community Integrity: In Community Raids, Explorers must remain respectful to fellow scouts. Toxic behavior will result in immediate "System Deactivation" (Account Suspension).

5. Termination of Link
The Explorer may terminate this agreement at any time by deactivating their account. Upon deactivation, the Lab will "Wipe" your bio-stats from the active grid, though some anonymized data may remain for system calibration.

1. "Ghost-Path" Augmented Reality (AR)
Instead of just looking at your phone to see where to go, users can use the AR View.

The Feature: When you hold your phone up, you see a glowing Neon Cyan line on the actual sidewalk in front of you (like a video game waymarker).

The "Lab" Twist: If you are racing your previous best time, you see a "Ghost Explorer" (a translucent silhouette) running ahead of you. To beat your "Personal Best," you have to physically overtake your ghost.

Why it‚Äôs great: It turns a boring walk into a high-stakes "Real World" race.

2. "Bio-Sync" Dynamic Music Engine
Music shouldn't just play; it should react to your body.

The Feature: The app connects to Spotify/Apple Music and uses an AI DJ to adjust the BPM (Beats Per Minute) of your music based on your heart rate and walking cadence.

The "Lab" Twist: If the Lab detects your heart rate dropping below the "Fat Burn Zone," the music automatically switches to a high-tempo track to push you back into the zone. When you enter the "Cool Down" phase, the music shifts to ambient, minimalist lo-fi.

Why it‚Äôs great: It creates a seamless "Flow State" where the audio matches your biological output.

3. "Terrain-Aware" Calorie Precision
Standard apps think walking on a flat treadmill is the same as walking on a forest trail. Path-Pulse shouldn't.

The Feature: Using the phone's barometer and GPS elevation data, the app identifies the surface type (sand, pavement, grass, or incline).

The "Lab" Twist: It adjusts your calorie burn in real-time. Walking in sand burns roughly 2x the calories of pavement. The Lab provides a "Terrain Difficulty Multiplier" in your Sunday Diagnostic Report.

Why it‚Äôs great: It satisfies the "Data Nerds" with extreme accuracy and rewards the "Warriors" for choosing harder paths.

4. "Predictive Fueling" (AI Meal Prep)
Instead of just logging what you already ate, the app tells you what you should eat for tomorrow.

The Feature: The app looks at your scheduled "Expedition" for tomorrow and your current recovery stats.

The "Lab" Twist: It sends a notification: "Tomorrow's 10-mile Expedition requires high glycogen. Recommendation: Increase complex carb intake by 20% tonight. Here is a 15-minute recipe for Sweet Potato Carbonara."

Why it‚Äôs great: it removes the "decision fatigue" for people trying to lose weight.

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

void main() => runApp(PathPulseApp());

class PathPulseApp extends StatelessWidget {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      title: 'Path-Pulse',
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      theme: ThemeData(
        brightness: Brightness.dark,
        scaffoldBackgroundColor: const Color(0xFF0B0E11), // Obsidian Black
        primaryColor: const Color(0xFF00F5FF), // Neon Cyan
        hintColor: const Color(0xFF39FF14), // Electric Lime
        fontFamily: 'JetBrainsMono', // Using a technical monospace font
      ),
      home: Dashboard(),
    );
  }
}

class Dashboard extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _DashboardState createState() => _DashboardState();
}

class _DashboardState extends State<Dashboard> {
  // Mock Data for "The Lab"
  double userWeight = 85.0; // kg
  double userHeight = 1.80; // meters
  int dailySteps = 8422;
  
  // Bio-Diagnostic Calculations
  double calculateBMI() => userWeight / (userHeight * userHeight);
  
  // Mifflin-St Jeor Equation (simplified for Male)
  double calculateBMR() => (10 * userWeight) + (6.25 * (userHeight * 100)) - (5 * 30) + 5;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: SafeArea(
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20.0),
          child: Column(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              _buildHeader(),
              const SizedBox(height: 40),
              _buildKineticRing(),
              const SizedBox(height: 40),
              _buildBioDiagnosticCard(),
              const Spacer(),
              _buildBottomNav(),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildHeader() {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
      children: [
        Column(
          crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          children: [
            Text("EXPLORER ID: PATHFINDER_01", 
                 style: TextStyle(color: Colors.grey, fontSize: 12)),
            Text("SYSTEM ACTIVE", 
                 style: TextStyle(color: Color(0xFF00F5FF), fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, fontSize: 18)),
          ],
        ),
        Icon(Icons.radar, color: Color(0xFF00F5FF), size: 30),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildKineticRing() {
    return Center(
      child: Stack(
        alignment: Alignment.center,
        children: [
          SizedBox(
            width: 200, height: 200,
            child: CircularProgressIndicator(
              value: dailySteps / 10000,
              strokeWidth: 8,
              backgroundColor: Colors.white10,
              valueColor: AlwaysStoppedAnimation<Color>(Color(0xFF39FF14)),
            ),
          ),
          Column(
            children: [
              Text("$dailySteps", style: TextStyle(fontSize: 40, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
              Text("KINETIC STEPS", style: TextStyle(color: Colors.grey, fontSize: 10)),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBioDiagnosticCard() {
    return Container(
      padding: EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.05),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(15),
        border: Border.all(color: Colors.white10),
      ),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          _dataRow("CURRENT BMI", calculateBMI().toStringAsFixed(1)),
          Divider(color: Colors.white10),
          _dataRow("BASE METABOLIC RATE", "${calculateBMR().toInt()} KCAL"),
          Divider(color: Colors.white10),
          _dataRow("SYSTEM STATUS", "OPTIMAL", color: Color(0xFF39FF14)),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _dataRow(String label, String value, {Color color = Colors.white}) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 8.0),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
        children: [
          Text(label, style: TextStyle(fontSize: 10, color: Colors.grey)),
          Text(value, style: TextStyle(fontSize: 14, color: color, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBottomNav() {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
      children: [
        Icon(Icons.map_outlined, color: Colors.grey),
        Icon(Icons.home_filled, color: Color(0xFF00F5FF)),
        Icon(Icons.restaurant_menu_outlined, color: Colors.grey),
      ],
    );
  }
}

üõ∞Ô∏è Phase 1: The Kinetic Map Overlay
To achieve the 40% Lab look, we aren't using standard Google Maps. We are using Mapbox because it allows for "Obsidian" vector styling and custom "Laser Trace" polyline rendering.

üõ†Ô∏è The Map Implementation (Flutter + Mapbox)
This module handles the GPS initialization and the drawing of the glowing route.

Dart
// pubspec.yaml dependency: mapbox_gl: ^0.16.0
import 'package:mapbox_gl/mapbox_gl.dart';

class KineticMap extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _KineticMapState createState() => _KineticMapState();
}

class _KineticMapState extends State<KineticMap> {
  MapboxMapController? mapController;

  // Obsidian Tactical Style URL (Custom Mapbox Style)
  final String obsidianStyle = "mapbox://styles/pathpulse/cl_obsidian_dark_v1";

  void _onMapCreated(MapboxMapController controller) {
    mapController = controller;
  }

  // The "Laser Trace" logic
  void _drawLaserRoute(List<LatLng> points) async {
    await mapController?.addLine(
      LineOptions(
        geometry: points,
        lineColor: "#00F5FF", // Neon Cyan
        lineWidth: 4.0,
        lineOpacity: 0.8,
        lineBlur: 2.0, // Creates the "Glow" effect
      ),
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MapboxMap(
      accessToken: "YOUR_MAPBOX_ACCESS_TOKEN",
      onMapCreated: _onMapCreated,
      initialCameraPosition: CameraPosition(target: LatLng(0, 0), zoom: 15),
      styleString: obsidianStyle,
      myLocationEnabled: true,
      myLocationTrackingMode: MyLocationTrackingMode.TrackingGPS,
    );
  }
}
ü•ó Phase 2: The Calorie/Meal Prep Engine
This module connects the Kinetic Burn (output) to the Fueling Protocol (input). It uses the "Terrain-Aware" logic we discussed.

üõ†Ô∏è The Fueling Logic
Dart
class FuelingEngine {
  // Terrain Multipliers
  static const double pavement = 1.0;
  static const double grass = 1.2;
  static const double sand = 2.1;

  double calculateActiveBurn(int steps, double terrainMultiplier) {
    // Basic metabolic formula for calories per step
    double baseBurnPerStep = 0.04; 
    return (steps * baseBurnPerStep) * terrainMultiplier;
  }

  // Predictive Fueling: Recommends protein/carbs based on next mission
  Map<String, String> getPredictiveMeal(double plannedDistanceKM) {
    if (plannedDistanceKM > 10) {
      return {
        "label": "High-Performance Protocol",
        "meal": "Complex Carbs + Lean Protein",
        "suggestion": "Quinoa bowl with Grilled Salmon"
      };
    } else {
      return {
        "label": "Recovery Protocol",
        "meal": "High Protein + Anti-Inflammatory",
        "suggestion": "Greek Yogurt with Chia & Walnuts"
      };
    }
  }
}
üéñÔ∏è Phase 3: The Leveling & XP System
This is the "Quest-Log" logic. It calculates experience points (XP) and handles the "Rank Up" triggers that change the UI and App Icon.

üõ†Ô∏è The Rank Controller
Dart
class RankController {
  int currentXP = 0;
  
  String getRankTitle(int level) {
    if (level < 10) return "RECRUIT";
    if (level < 25) return "SCOUT";
    if (level < 50) return "VANGUARD";
    if (level < 75) return "BIO-COMMANDER";
    return "APEX PATHFINDER";
  }

  // Calculate Level based on XP (Logarithmic progression)
  int getLevel() {
    // Every level requires 10% more XP than the last
    return (0.1 * (currentXP ^ 0.5)).toInt() + 1;
  }

  // Logic to trigger App Icon Change (Requires MethodChannel for native iOS/Android)
  void updateAppIcon(int level) {
    if (level == 100) {
      // Logic to swap icon to 'holographic_icon.png'
      print("System Update: Holographic Icon Unlocked.");
    }
  }
}

Dart
class DiagnosticReport {
  final double weightStart;
  final double weightEnd;
  final int totalSteps;
  final List<double> terrainMultipliers;

  DiagnosticReport({required this.weightStart, required this.weightEnd, required this.totalSteps, required this.terrainMultipliers});

  // Calculate the average terrain difficulty for the week
  double get averageDifficulty {
    return terrainMultipliers.reduce((a, b) => a + b) / terrainMultipliers.length;
  }

  // Generate a "System Verdict"
  String getVerdict() {
    double delta = weightStart - weightEnd;
    if (delta > 0.5) return "OPTIMAL EVOLUTION: PROTOCOL EXCEEDED";
    if (delta > 0) return "STABLE PROGRESS: MAINTAIN VELOCITY";
    return "STAGNATION DETECTED: ADJUST FUELING PROTOCOL";
  }
}

Dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:math';

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
// 1. SYSTEM ENTRY & THEME (The Obsidian Aesthetic)
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
void main() => runApp(PathPulseTitan());

class PathPulseTitan extends StatelessWidget {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      theme: ThemeData(
        brightness: Brightness.dark,
        scaffoldBackgroundColor: const Color(0xFF0B0E11), // Obsidian Black
        primaryColor: const Color(0xFF00F5FF), // Neon Cyan
        colorScheme: ColorScheme.dark(
          secondary: const Color(0xFF39FF14), // Electric Lime
        ),
        textTheme: const TextTheme(
          bodyMedium: TextStyle(fontFamily: 'Courier', color: Colors.white70),
        ),
      ),
      home: const MainCommandCenter(),
    );
  }
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
// 2. GLOBAL STATE MANAGER (The Brain)
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
class SystemCommander extends ChangeNotifier {
  int level = 1;
  int xp = 0;
  double weight = 85.0; // kg
  int dailySteps = 7540;
  bool isMissionActive = false;

  void addXP(int amount) {
    xp += amount;
    // Logarithmic Leveling Logic
    level = (0.1 * sqrt(xp)).toInt() + 1;
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void toggleMission() {
    isMissionActive = !isMissionActive;
    notifyListeners();
  }
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
// 3. LOGIC ENGINES (Fueling & Bio-Diagnostics)
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
class LabEngine {
  static double calculateBMI(double weight, double height) => weight / (height * height);

  static Map<String, dynamic> getFuelingProtocol(int steps, double terrainDifficulty) {
    double caloriesBurned = (steps * 0.04) * terrainDifficulty;
    return {
      "burn": caloriesBurned.toInt(),
      "suggestion": steps > 10000 ? "High-Carb Recovery" : "Baseline Protein",
      "status": "CALIBRATED"
    };
  }
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
// 4. UI COMPONENTS (Dashboard & HUD)
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
class MainCommandCenter extends StatefulWidget {
  const MainCommandCenter({super.key});

  @override
  State<MainCommandCenter> createState() => _MainCommandCenterState();
}

class _MainCommandCenterState extends State<MainCommandCenter> {
  final SystemCommander cmd = SystemCommander();

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: SafeArea(
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20, vertical: 10),
          child: Column(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              _buildTopBar(),
              const SizedBox(height: 30),
              _buildKineticGauges(),
              const SizedBox(height: 20),
              _buildMissionControl(),
              const SizedBox(height: 20),
              _buildBioDiagnosticPanel(),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTopBar() {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
      children: [
        Column(
          crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          children: [
            const Text("PATHFINDER_v1.0", style: TextStyle(fontSize: 10, letterSpacing: 2)),
            Text("LEVEL ${cmd.level} ${cmd.level >= 50 ? 'ELITE' : 'SCOUT'}", 
                 style: const TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Color(0xFF00F5FF))),
          ],
        ),
        const CircleAvatar(backgroundColor: Colors.white10, child: Icon(Icons.person, color: Colors.white)),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildKineticGauges() {
    return Container(
      height: 180,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.03),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
        border: Border.all(color: Colors.white10),
      ),
      child: Center(
        child: Column(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            Text("${cmd.dailySteps}", style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 48, fontWeight: FontWeight.w900, color: Color(0xFF39FF14))),
            const Text("KINETIC DATA PULSE", style: TextStyle(fontSize: 10, color: Colors.grey)),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildMissionControl() {
    return InkWell(
      onTap: () => setState(() => cmd.toggleMission()),
      child: Container(
        width: double.infinity,
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: cmd.isMissionActive ? const Color(0xFF00F5FF).withOpacity(0.1) : Colors.white10,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(15),
          border: Border.all(color: cmd.isMissionActive ? const Color(0xFF00F5FF) : Colors.white24),
        ),
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            Icon(cmd.isMissionActive ? Icons.radar : Icons.play_arrow, color: cmd.isMissionActive ? const Color(0xFF00F5FF) : Colors.white),
            const SizedBox(width: 10),
            Text(cmd.isMissionActive ? "INITIALIZING GHOST-PATH..." : "START EXPEDITION", 
                 style: const TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBioDiagnosticPanel() {
    var protocol = LabEngine.getFuelingProtocol(cmd.dailySteps, 1.2);
    return Expanded(
      child: ListView(
        children: [
          const Text("DIAGNOSTICS", style: TextStyle(fontSize: 12, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
          const SizedBox(height: 10),
          _diagnosticRow("METABOLIC BURN", "${protocol['burn']} KCAL"),
          _diagnosticRow("FUELING PROTOCOL", "${protocol['suggestion']}"),
          _diagnosticRow("SYSTEM STATUS", "OPTIMAL", color: const Color(0xFF39FF14)),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _diagnosticRow(String title, String val, {Color color = Colors.white}) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 12),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
        children: [
          Text(title, style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.grey, fontSize: 12)),
          Text(val, style: TextStyle(color: color, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, fontSize: 12)),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

  contents: import 'dart:math';

/// Path-Pulse core logic: Bio-Diagnostics, Fueling, Rank.
class LabEngine {
  static double calculateBMI(double weightKg, double heightM) =>
      weightKg / (heightM * heightM);

  /// Mifflin-St Jeor BMR (male; use -161 for female).
  static double calculateBMR(double weightKg, double heightCm, int age, {bool isMale = true}) {
    return (10 * weightKg) + (6.25 * heightCm) - (5 * age) + (isMale ? 5 : -161);
  }

  /// Terrain multipliers for calorie precision.
  static const double terrainPavement = 1.0;
  static const double terrainGrass = 1.2;
  static const double terrainSand = 2.1;

  static Map<String, dynamic> getFuelingProtocol(int steps, double terrainMultiplier) {
    const double baseBurnPerStep = 0.04;
    double caloriesBurned = (steps * baseBurnPerStep) * terrainMultiplier;
    return {
      'burn': caloriesBurned.round(),
      'suggestion': steps > 10000 ? 'High-Carb Recovery' : 'Baseline Protein',
      'status': 'CALIBRATED',
    };
  }

  /// Predictive meal suggestion based on planned distance (km).
  static Map<String, String> getPredictiveMeal(double plannedDistanceKm) {
    if (plannedDistanceKm > 10) {
      return {
        'label': 'High-Performance Protocol',
        'meal': 'Complex Carbs + Lean Protein',
        'suggestion': 'Quinoa bowl with Grilled Salmon',
      };
    }
    return {
      'label': 'Recovery Protocol',
      'meal': 'High Protein + Anti-Inflammatory',
      'suggestion': 'Greek Yogurt with Chia & Walnuts',
    };
  }
}

/// Rank / level progression (1‚Äì100).
class RankController {
  static String getRankTitle(int level) {
    if (level < 10) return 'RECRUIT';
    if (level < 25) return 'SCOUT';
    if (level < 50) return 'VANGUARD';
    if (level < 75) return 'BIO-COMMANDER';
    return 'APEX PATHFINDER';
  }

  /// Level from total XP (logarithmic).
  static int getLevelFromXP(int totalXP) {
    if (totalXP <= 0) return 1;
    return (0.1 * sqrt(totalXP)).floor() + 1;
  }

  static String getBadgeName(int level) {
    if (level <= 10) return 'The Spark Core';
    if (level <= 25) return 'The Vector Wing';
    if (level <= 50) return 'The Kinetic Shield';
    if (level <= 75) return 'The Helix Prime';
    if (level < 100) return 'The Global Sentinel';
    return 'The Apex Origin';
  }
}

/// Weekly diagnostic report data.
class DiagnosticReport {
  final double weightStart;
  final double weightEnd;
  final int totalSteps;
  final List<double> terrainMultipliers;

  DiagnosticReport({
    required this.weightStart,
    required this.weightEnd,
    required this.totalSteps,
    required this.terrainMultipliers,
  });

  double get averageDifficulty =>
      terrainMultipliers.isEmpty ? 1.0 : terrainMultipliers.reduce((a, b) => a + b) / terrainMultipliers.length;

  String getVerdict() {
    double delta = weightStart - weightEnd;
    if (delta > 0.5) return 'OPTIMAL EVOLUTION: PROTOCOL EXCEEDED';
    if (delta > 0) return 'STABLE PROGRESS: MAINTAIN VELOCITY';
    return 'STAGNATION DETECTED: ADJUST FUELING PROTOCOL';
  }
}

  path: c:\Users\HOME\.cursor\projects\2026 project\Path Pulse file\path_pulse\lib\state\system_commander.dart
  contents: import 'dart:math';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';
import '../engine.dart';

/// Global state: level, XP, mission, oath, profile.
class SystemCommander extends ChangeNotifier {
  bool oathAccepted = false;
  int xp = 0;
  double weight = 85.0; // kg
  double height = 1.80; // m
  int age = 30;
  bool isMale = true;
  int dailySteps = 7540;
  bool isMissionActive = false;
  String explorerId = 'PATHFINDER_01';

  int get level => RankController.getLevelFromXP(xp);
  String get rankTitle => RankController.getRankTitle(level);
  double get bmi => LabEngine.calculateBMI(weight, height);
  double get bmr => LabEngine.calculateBMR(weight, height * 100, age, isMale: isMale);

  void acceptOath() {
    oathAccepted = true;
    explorerId = 'PATHFINDER_${100 + xp % 900}X';
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void addXP(int amount) {
    xp += amount;
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void toggleMission() {
    isMissionActive = !isMissionActive;
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void updateSteps(int steps) {
    dailySteps = steps;
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void updateProfile({double? w, double? h, int? a, bool? male}) {
    if (w != null) weight = w;
    if (h != null) height = h;
    if (a != null) age = a;
    if (male != null) isMale = male;
    notifyListeners();
  }
}

**Tagline:** Trace Your Path. Pulse Your Progress.

**Concept:** A high-tech "Bio-Explorer" utility that fuses GPS storytelling with clinical health analytics for Android and iOS.

---

## 1. Visual & Aesthetic Identity

- **Vibe:** 40% High-Tech Lab / 20% Minimalist Zen / 40% Futuristic Quest
- **UI/UX:** Obsidian Dark Mode (`#0B0E11`), Neon Cyan (`#00F5FF`), Electric Lime (`#39FF14`)
- **Key Icon:** The Pulse-Pointer ‚Äî GPS pin integrated with a heartbeat waveform
- **Interface:** Glass-morphism layers, monospaced technical typography

---

## 2. Core Tracking & GPS

- **Tactical Trace:** Real-time GPS on a dark-vector map
- **Kinetic Time-Lapse:** 3D wireframe video of each walk with data call-outs (elevation, speed, peak HR)
- **Step Quality Index:** Cadence analysis ‚Äî "Passive Steps" vs "Power Steps"

---

## 3. Bio-Diagnostic Suite (The Lab)

- **Body Composition Matrix:** BMI + 3D wireframe silhouette evolution
- **Metabolic Engine:** BMR, "Fat-to-Fuel" efficiency from walk intensity
- **Weekly Diagnostic Report:** "Declassified" mission summary (PDF/Video) every Sunday

---

## 4. Metabolic Fueling (Calorie & Meal Prep)

- **Fuel Gauge:** Real-time calorie counter (BMR + active burn vs intake)
- **Precision Meal Prep:** Ingredient scanner, Protocol recipes by expedition intensity
- **Hydration Logic:** Water needs from GPS-tracked route/sweat data

---

## 5. Quest-Log (Gamification)

- **Expeditions:** Missions like "Operation: Metabolism Spike", "The Urban Ridge"
- **Rank Progression:** Level 1 (Civilian) ‚Üí Level 100 (Apex Pathfinder), map skins, Lab features
- **Community Raids:** Co-op step challenges with friends

---

## 6. Business & Tech

- **Monetization:** Free tier (steps, basic BMI, standard maps); **Path-Pulse Pro** ($9.99/mo): advanced analytics, unlimited time-lapses, full Meal Prep/Calorie suite
- **Tech Stack:** Mapbox SDK, HealthKit/Health Connect, FFmpeg (video), AI for meal/walk protocols

---

## 7. Titan Update (Advanced Systems)

- **AR Ghost-Path:** Race your "past self" overlay in the real world
- **Bio-Sync Audio:** Music BPM aligned to heart rate zones
- **Terrain-Aware Calorie Precision:** Surface multiplier (sand, grass, pavement)
- **Predictive Fueling AI:** Meal suggestions based on next day‚Äôs expedition

---

## 8. Next Steps for Development

1. Prototype the Time-Lapse Engine (3D wireframe, shareable).
2. Integrate Calorie/Bio-Database with BMI trend graphs.
3. Beta launch "Operation: First Step" (30-day challenge).

  contents: # Path-Pulse: The Explorer‚Äôs Oath

**Subject:** System Access & Biological Data Protocols  
**Status:** REQUIRED FOR INITIALIZATION

By tapping **"INITIALIZE SYSTEM"**, you (the **Explorer**) agree to the following protocols and terms of service.

---

## 1. The Bio-Data Protocol (Privacy)

- **Data Collection:** You authorize the Lab to sync with your device‚Äôs health sensors (GPS, Heart Rate, Biometrics).
- **Encryption:** Your biological data is encrypted and used solely for Diagnostic Reports and Metabolic Fueling plans.
- **Social Sharing:** Any Tactical Time-Lapses or Mission Briefings you share are at your discretion; once shared, they are visible on the "Global Grid."

## 2. Kinetic Liability (Safety)

- **Situational Awareness:** Maintain full awareness of your surroundings. Do not focus on the Tactical Overlay while crossing intersections or hazardous terrain.
- **Physical Limits:** Expeditions and Protocols are suggestions. If your body signals pain or exhaustion, stop. Path-Pulse is not liable for over-exertion or environmental hazards.

## 3. The Fueling & Nutrition Directive

- **Not Medical Advice:** Metabolic Fueling and Meal Prep are based on general nutrition and your logged data. They do not replace a doctor or nutritionist.
- **Accuracy:** Calorie counting is an estimate; the Lab is only as accurate as the data you input.

## 4. Code of the Global Grid (Conduct)

- **Fair Play:** Do not use vehicles (cars, bikes, drones) to spoof GPS data for rank.
- **Community Integrity:** In Community Raids, remain respectful. Toxic behavior may result in account suspension.

## 5. Termination of Link

- You may terminate this agreement at any time by deactivating your account. Upon deactivation, the Lab will remove your bio-stats from the active grid; some anonymized data may remain for system calibration.

---

## Consent Interaction

**"DO YOU ACCEPT THE MISSION AND THE RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXPLORER'S OATH?"**

- **[ INITIALIZE LINK ]**  
- **[ ABORT MISSION ]**

  contents: # The Initialization Manifesto: Why Path-Pulse?

## The Era of "Shame-Tracking" is Over

For the last decade, fitness apps have treated us like entries in a spreadsheet. Red bars, "broken streaks," and leaderboard shaming. They turned health into a chore and movement into a transaction.

By 2026, we've had enough. We don't need another digital nag; we need a **Biological Operating System**.

---

## The Lab vs. The Gym

We didn't build Path-Pulse to help you "jog." We built it to help you **explore**.

We believe your body is the most sophisticated hardware on the planet. Every walk, run, or climb is a tactical expedition into your own potential. Why should your data look like a 2012 bank statement when it could look like a declassified tactical briefing?

*"We are moving from 'What did I do?' to 'Who am I becoming?' Path-Pulse isn't a tracker; it's a mirror reflecting your evolution in 4K neon."*

---

## The Three Pillars of the Grid

1. **Precision Without Emotion** ‚Äî The Lab doesn't judge; it calibrates. Data is objective. Our Terrain-Aware Engine credits the grit of sand and the steepness of the hill where legacy apps see flat lines.

2. **Movement as Storytelling** ‚Äî Your path is unique. Tactical Time-Lapses and AR Ghost-Paths turn your morning route into a cinematic event. If it isn't visually stunning, it isn't Path-Pulse.

3. **Proactive Evolution** ‚Äî We're done with only looking backward. Predictive Fueling tells you how to prepare for tomorrow's mission today. We remove decision fatigue so you can focus on the path.

---

## The Grid is Waiting

We aren't looking for "users." We are recruiting **Pathfinders**. Those who want to see the wireframe of the world, race their own ghosts, and master their biology through data and design.

The old world of fitness was about fitting in. **The New Protocol is about standing out.**

**Initialize the Grid. Take the Explorer's Oath.**

  path: c:\Users\HOME\.cursor\projects\2026 project\Path Pulse file\marketing\COMPETITIVE_ANALYSIS.md
  contents: # Path-Pulse Competitive Battle Card (2026)

## Feature Comparison

| Feature            | Path-Pulse              | Strava              | MyFitnessPal       | Whoop / Oura      |
|--------------------|-------------------------|---------------------|--------------------|-------------------|
| Primary Vibe       | Tactical Lab            | Social Network      | Digital Logbook    | Recovery Monitor  |
| Movement Tracking  | Terrain-Aware (Tm)      | GPS + Elevation     | Basic Steps        | Passive HR / Sleep|
| Social Flex        | 3D Tactical Time-Lapses | Static Maps/Photos  | Text Logs          | Private Sharing   |
| User Motivation    | Level 1‚Äì100 Exploration | Leaderboard Shame   | Goal Shame (Red)   | Readiness Scores  |
| Key Innovation     | AR Ghost-Path Racing    | Segments & Crowns   | Barcode Scan       | Wearable Hardware |
| UI                 | Obsidian Minimalism     | High-contrast Orange| Ad-heavy, Crowded  | Minimalist App    |

---

## Why Path-Pulse Wins

1. **From Shame to Discovery** ‚Äî Strava/MFP rely on streaks and leaderboards ‚Üí burnout. Path-Pulse: objective Lab framing ("Bio-Baseline Stable. Fueling protocol adjusted.").

2. **Terrain Multiplier (Tm)** ‚Äî Most apps treat 5 km treadmill = 5 km beach. Path-Pulse gives hidden credit (e.g. sand = 2.1√ó). Data Nerds choose the hard path because the app validates it.

3. **Visual Prestige** ‚Äî Legacy shares look like utility tools. Path-Pulse 3D Time-Lapses and AR Ghost clips are shareable, sci-fi, and position the user as a "Pathfinder."

---

## Tactical Strike

- **Vs Strava:** More immersive, solo-focused; race *your* Ghost on *your* street.
- **Vs MyFitnessPal:** Predictive Fueling instead of manual-entry headache.
- **Vs Whoop:** Elite-level biometric insights using phone + existing watch, no mandatory hardware.

**Verdict:** Path-Pulse wins by making health an *experience*‚Äîexploration and biology‚Äînot another to-do list.

[Tool call] Write
  path: c:\Users\HOME\.cursor\projects\2026 project\Path Pulse file\DEVELOPER_HANDOVER_SUMMARY.md
  contents: # Developer Handover: Project Path-Pulse

**Version:** 1.0 (Titan Build)  
**Objective:** High-performance lifestyle app fusing GPS storytelling, clinical bio-analytics, and AR gamification.

---

## 1. Technical Architecture (Stack)

| Layer      | Choice |
|-----------|--------|
| Frontend  | Flutter (cross-platform iOS/Android) for minimalist UI. |
| Maps      | Mapbox SDK ‚Äî custom "Obsidian" GL styles, Terrain-RGB for elevation. |
| Health    | Apple HealthKit / Google Health Connect. |
| Video     | FFmpeg (server or local) to render GPS paths into 3D wireframe time-lapses. |
| AR        | ARKit (iOS) / ARCore (Android) for Ghost-Path overlay. |

---

## 2. Core Functional Modules

**Module A: Kinetic Engine (GPS/Motion)**  
- Real-time location + Terrain-Awareness.  
- Barometer/altimeter for Terrain Multiplier (Tm) in calorie math.  
- Smoothed polylines for "Laser Trace" visuals.

**Module B: Bio-Diagnostic Lab**  
- BMI, BMR (Mifflin‚ÄìSt Jeor), Fat-to-Fuel logic.  
- Weekly PDF/MP4 Diagnostic Report generation.

**Module C: Bio-Sync Audio**  
- Spotify/Apple Music API.  
- Dynamic playlist by real-time HR (BPM) zones.

**Module D: Metabolic Fueling**  
- Recipe DB + Scanner API (e.g. Nutritionix).  
- Predictive AI: meal suggestions from next day‚Äôs scheduled expedition.

---

## 3. UI/UX Specs

- **Theme:** Obsidian Dark `#0B0E11`, Neon Cyan `#00F5FF`, Electric Lime `#39FF14`.  
- **Design:** Glass-morphism, monospaced fonts for technical data.  
- **Gamification:** Level 1‚Äì100 with dynamic app icon asset swap by level.

---

## 4. MVP Milestones

1. **Sprint 1:** Auth, Explorer‚Äôs Oath onboarding, basic step/GPS tracking.  
2. **Sprint 2:** Bio-Diagnostic dashboard, BMI/BMR trend graphs.  
3. **Sprint 3:** Automated 3D time-lapse video generation.  
4. **Sprint 4:** Meal Prep/Calorie counter, AR Ghost V1.

---

## 5. Key API & Permissions

- **Location:** Always-on (route monitoring).  
- **Biometrics:** Read/Write Heart Rate, Weight, Energy Expended.  
- **Camera:** AR Ghost-Path and meal/barcode scanning.

---

## 6. Formulae (Lab Logic)

- **BMI:** `BMI = mass_kg / height_m¬≤`
- **BMR:** Mifflin‚ÄìSt Jeor equation.
- **Terrain burn:** `TotalBurn = (BaseBurn √ó Duration) √ó Tm`  
  (e.g. Sand ‚âà 2.1√ó, Grass ‚âà 1.2√ó, Pavement = 1.0√ó)

This document is the logic, math, and aesthetic baseline for development.

**Tagline:** Don't just walk. Trace your evolution.

Path-Pulse is a Bio-Explorer utility that turns every step into a tactical mission. It combines terrain-aware GPS, metabolic diagnostics (BMI/BMR, fat-to-fuel efficiency), 3D Tactical Time-Lapses, and optional AR Ghost-Path racing. Built for Data Nerds, Social Butterflies, and Weight-Loss Warriors‚Äîwith an Obsidian Lab aesthetic and a Level 1‚Äì100 quest system.

For a Level 10 Scout on "Operation: Metabolism Spike." Balances BMI baseline with kinetic output.

## Day 1: Calibration Day (Low-Carb / High Protein)

**Goal:** Stabilize blood sugar, prep for fat-to-fuel conversion.

| Time | Station | Meal |
|------|---------|------|
| 08:00 | Fueling Station 1 | Two poached eggs over saut√©ed spinach and sliced avocado. |
| 13:00 | Fueling Station 2 | Grilled lemon-herb chicken breast, "Green Grid" salad (cucumber, kale, pumpkin seeds). |
| 16:00 | Kinetic Boost | Handful of raw almonds. |
| 19:00 | System Recovery | Baked salmon, roasted asparagus, cauliflower rice. |

**Protocol:** 2.5 L H‚ÇÇO.

---

## Day 2: Expedition Day (Performance Carbs)

**Goal:** Fuel for a scheduled 5-mile Power Walk.

| Time | Station | Meal |
|------|---------|------|
| 08:00 | Fueling Station 1 | Steel-cut oats, blueberries, scoop of whey or plant protein. |
| 13:00 | Fueling Station 2 | Quinoa bowl with black beans, bell peppers, lean ground turkey. |
| 15:00 | Pre-Mission | One medium banana (quick glycogen). |
| 19:00 | System Recovery | Lean beef stir-fry with broccoli, snap peas, small portion brown rice. |

**Protocol:** 3.0 L H‚ÇÇO (increased for mission recovery).

---

## Day 3: Reconstruction Day (Anti-Inflammatory)

**Goal:** Repair muscle, optimize BMI trendline.

| Time | Station | Meal |
|------|---------|------|
| 08:00 | Fueling Station 1 | Greek yogurt (plain), chia seeds, walnuts. |
| 13:00 | Fueling Station 2 | Tuna salad (Greek yogurt instead of mayo) in large romaine leaves. |
| 16:00 | Kinetic Boost | Celery sticks with a small amount of almond butter. |
| 19:00 | System Recovery | "Lab Special" ‚Äî Roasted skinless chicken thigh, sweet potato, steamed zucchini. |

**Protocol:** 2.5 L H‚ÇÇO. (Sweet potato magnesium aids Kinetic Recovery.)

import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';

/// Global state: level, XP, mission, oath, profile.
class SystemCommander extends ChangeNotifier {
  bool oathAccepted = false;
  int xp = 0;
  double weight = 85.0; // kg
  double height = 1.80; // m
  int age = 30;
  bool isMale = true;
  int dailySteps = 7540;

  int get level => RankController.getLevelFromXP(xp);
  String get rankTitle => RankController.getRankTitle(level);
  double get bmi => LabEngine.calculateBMI(weight, height);
  double get bmr => LabEngine.calculateBMR(weight, height * 100, age, isMale: isMale);

  void acceptOath() {
    oathAccepted = true;
    explorerId = 'PATHFINDER_${100 + xp % 900}X';
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void addXP(int amount) {
    xp += amount;
    notifyListeners();

    isMissionActive = !isMissionActive;
    notifyListeners();

    if (h != null) height = h;

    notifyListeners();

}
  new_string: import 'dart:math';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import '../engine.dart';
import 'package:latlong2/latlong.dart';

/// Global state: level, XP, mission, oath, profile, route.
class SystemCommander extends ChangeNotifier {
  bool oathAccepted = false;
  int xp = 0;
  double weight = 85.0; // kg
  double height = 1.80; // m
  int age = 30;
  bool isMale = true;
  int dailySteps = 7540;
  bool isMissionActive = false;
  String explorerId = 'PATHFINDER_01';
  List<LatLng> routePoints = [];
  LatLng? currentPosition;

  static const _keyWeight = 'pp_weight';
  static const _keyHeight = 'pp_height';
  static const _keyAge = 'pp_age';
  static const _keyMale = 'pp_male';
  static const _keyOath = 'pp_oath';
  static const _keyXP = 'pp_xp';

  int get level => RankController.getLevelFromXP(xp);
  String get rankTitle => RankController.getRankTitle(level);
  double get bmi => LabEngine.calculateBMI(weight, height);
  double get bmr => LabEngine.calculateBMR(weight, height * 100, age, isMale: isMale);

  Future<void> loadFromStorage() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    weight = prefs.getDouble(_keyWeight) ?? weight;
    height = prefs.getDouble(_keyHeight) ?? height;
    age = prefs.getInt(_keyAge) ?? age;
    isMale = prefs.getBool(_keyMale) ?? isMale;
    oathAccepted = prefs.getBool(_keyOath) ?? false;
    xp = prefs.getInt(_keyXP) ?? 0;
    notifyListeners();
  }

  Future<void> saveProfile() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setDouble(_keyWeight, weight);
    await prefs.setDouble(_keyHeight, height);
    await prefs.setInt(_keyAge, age);
    await prefs.setBool(_keyMale, isMale);
    notifyListeners();
  }

  Future<void> saveOathAndXP() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setBool(_keyOath, oathAccepted);
    await prefs.setInt(_keyXP, xp);
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void acceptOath() {
    oathAccepted = true;
    explorerId = 'PATHFINDER_${100 + xp % 900}X';
    saveOathAndXP();
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void addXP(int amount) {
    xp += amount;
    saveOathAndXP();
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void toggleMission() {
    isMissionActive = !isMissionActive;
    if (!isMissionActive) {
      routePoints = [];
    }
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void updateSteps(int steps) {
    dailySteps = steps;
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void updateProfile({double? w, double? h, int? a, bool? male}) {
    if (w != null) weight = w;
    if (h != null) height = h;
    if (a != null) age = a;
    if (male != null) isMale = male;
    saveProfile();
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void setCurrentPosition(LatLng? pos) {
    currentPosition = pos;
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void appendRoutePoint(LatLng point) {
    routePoints = [...routePoints, point];
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void clearRoute() {
    routePoints = [];
    notifyListeners();
  }
}

import 'package:provider/provider.dart';

class ProfileScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const ProfileScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<ProfileScreen> createState() => _ProfileScreenState();
}

class _ProfileScreenState extends State<ProfileScreen> {
  late TextEditingController _weightCtrl;
  late TextEditingController _heightCtrl;
  late TextEditingController _ageCtrl;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    final cmd = Provider.of<SystemCommander>(context, listen: false);
    _weightCtrl = TextEditingController(text: cmd.weight.toStringAsFixed(1));
    _heightCtrl = TextEditingController(text: cmd.height.toStringAsFixed(2));
    _ageCtrl = TextEditingController(text: '${cmd.age}');
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _weightCtrl.dispose();
    _heightCtrl.dispose();
    _ageCtrl.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Consumer<SystemCommander>(
      builder: (context, cmd, _) {
        return Scaffold(
          body: SafeArea(
            child: Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24, vertical: 20),
              child: ListView(
                children: [
                  const Text(
                    'PHYSICAL SPECS',
                    style: TextStyle(

                        child: _sexChip(context, cmd, false, 'Female'),
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 32),
                  SizedBox(
                    height: 52,
                    child: ElevatedButton(
                      onPressed: () => _save(context, cmd),
                      style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
                        backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF00F5FF),

  Widget _field(String label, TextEditingController ctrl, {String? hint, TextInputType? keyboardType}) {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
      children: [
        Text(label, style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.grey, fontSize: 12)),
        const SizedBox(height: 6),
        TextField(

            hintText: hint,
            hintStyle: TextStyle(color: Colors.grey.shade600),
            filled: true,
            fillColor: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.06),
            border: OutlineInputBorder(
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
              borderSide: BorderSide(color: Colors.white24),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _sexChip(BuildContext context, SystemCommander cmd, bool value, String label) {
    final selected = cmd.isMale == value;
    return InkWell(
      onTap: () => cmd.updateProfile(male: value),
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 14),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: selected ? const Color(0xFF00F5FF).withOpacity(0.15) : Colors.white10,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
          border: Border.all(
            color: selected ? const Color(0xFF00F5FF) : Colors.white24,
          ),
        ),
        child: Center(
          child: Text(
            label,
            style: TextStyle(
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              color: selected ? const Color(0xFF00F5FF) : Colors.white70,
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _row(String label, String value) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 4),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
        children: [
          Text(label, style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.grey, fontSize: 12)),
          Text(value, style: const TextStyle(color: Color(0xFF39FF14), fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  void _save(BuildContext context, SystemCommander cmd) {
    final w = double.tryParse(_weightCtrl.text);
    final h = double.tryParse(_heightCtrl.text);
    final a = int.tryParse(_ageCtrl.text);
    if (w != null && w > 0 && w < 300) cmd.updateProfile(w: w);
    if (h != null && h > 0 && h < 3) cmd.updateProfile(h: h);
    if (a != null && a > 0 && a < 150) cmd.updateProfile(a: a);
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: const Text('Baseline saved. Lab recalculated.'),
        backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF39FF14).withOpacity(0.9),
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
      ),
    );
  }
}

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:provider/provider.dart';

import 'package:geolocator/geolocator.dart';
import 'package:permission_handler/permission_handler.dart';
import '../state/system_commander.dart';

class MapScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const MapScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<MapScreen> createState() => _MapScreenState();
}

class _MapScreenState extends State<MapScreen> {
  final MapController _mapController = MapController();
  StreamSubscription<Position>? _positionSubscription;
  static const LatLng _defaultCenter = LatLng(51.5, -0.09); // London fallback

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _requestLocationAndListen();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _positionSubscription?.cancel();
    super.dispose();
  }

  Future<void> _requestLocationAndListen() async {
    final status = await Permission.location.request();
    if (!status.isGranted) return;
    final cmd = context.read<SystemCommander>();
    if (!cmd.isMissionActive) {
      final pos = await Geolocator.getCurrentPosition(
        desiredAccuracy: LocationAccuracy.high,
      ).catchError((_) => null);
      if (pos != null && mounted) {
        cmd.setCurrentPosition(LatLng(pos.latitude, pos.longitude));
      }
    }
    _positionSubscription = Geolocator.getPositionStream(
      locationSettings: const LocationSettings(accuracy: LocationAccuracy.high),
    ).listen((Position pos) {
      if (!mounted) return;
      final c = context.read<SystemCommander>();
      c.setCurrentPosition(LatLng(pos.latitude, pos.longitude));
      if (c.isMissionActive) {
        c.appendRoutePoint(LatLng(pos.latitude, pos.longitude));
      }
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Consumer<SystemCommander>(
      builder: (context, cmd, _) {
        final center = cmd.currentPosition ?? _defaultCenter;
        return Scaffold(
          body: FlutterMap(
            mapController: _mapController,
            options: MapOptions(
              initialCenter: center,
              initialZoom: 15,
              onTap: (_, __) {},
            ),
            children: [
              TileLayer(
                urlTemplate: 'https://{s}.basemaps.cartocdn.com/dark_all/{z}/{x}/{y}{r}.png',
                subdomains: const ['a', 'b', 'c', 'd'],
              ),
              if (cmd.routePoints.isNotEmpty)
                PolylineLayer(
                  polylines: [
                    Polyline(
                      points: cmd.routePoints,
                      strokeWidth: 5,
                      color: const Color(0xFF00F5FF),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              if (cmd.currentPosition != null)
                MarkerLayer(
                  markers: [
                    Marker(
                      point: cmd.currentPosition!,
                      width: 24,
                      height: 24,
                      child: const Icon(
                        Icons.location_on,
                        color: Color(0xFF39FF14),
                        size: 24,
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
            ],
          ),
          floatingActionButton: Column(
            mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
            children: [
              if (cmd.currentPosition != null)
                FloatingActionButton.small(
                  heroTag: 'center',
                  onPressed: () {
                    _mapController.move(cmd.currentPosition!, 16);
                  },
                  backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF0B0E11),
                  child: const Icon(Icons.my_location, color: Color(0xFF00F5FF)),
                ),
              const SizedBox(height: 8),
              FloatingActionButton.extended(
                heroTag: 'mission',
                onPressed: () => cmd.toggleMission(),
                backgroundColor: cmd.isMissionActive
                    ? const Color(0xFFFF3131)
                    : const Color(0xFF00F5FF),
                icon: Icon(
                  cmd.isMissionActive ? Icons.stop : Icons.play_arrow,
                  color: const Color(0xFF0B0E11),
                ),
                label: Text(
                  cmd.isMissionActive ? 'STOP EXPEDITION' : 'START EXPEDITION',
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: Color(0xFF0B0E11),
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        );
      },
    );
  }

class _AppLoaderState extends State<_AppLoader> {
  bool _loaded = false;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    WidgetsBinding.instance.addPostFrameCallback((_) async {
      await context.read<SystemCommander>().loadFromStorage();

      );

    return Consumer<SystemCommander>(
      builder: (context, cmd, _) {
        if (!cmd.oathAccepted) {
          return const OnboardingOathScreen();
        }
        return const MainShell();
      },
    );
  }

  path: c:\Users\HOME\.cursor\projects\2026 project\Path Pulse file\path_pulse\PERMISSIONS.md
  contents: # Path-Pulse ‚Äî Required permissions

After you run `flutter create .` (or if you already have `android/` and `ios/`), add these so the map and expedition tracking work.

## Android

In **android/app/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml**, inside `<manifest>`, add:

```xml
<uses-permission android:name="android.permission.ACCESS_FINE_LOCATION" />
<uses-permission android:name="android.permission.ACCESS_COARSE_LOCATION" />
```

## iOS

In **ios/Runner/Info.plist**, inside `<dict>`, add:

```xml
<key>NSLocationWhenInUseUsageDescription</key>
<string>Path-Pulse needs location to record your route and show the tactical map.</string>
<key>NSLocationAlwaysAndWhenInUseUsageDescription</key>
<string>Path-Pulse uses location to track your expedition and draw the laser trace.</string>
```

Then run:

```bash
flutter pub get
flutter run
```

Summary of what‚Äôs in place:

---

## Sprint 1 done

### 1. **Profile screen**
- **Physical specs:** Weight (kg), height (m), age, sex (Male/Female).
- **Save baseline** updates `SystemCommander` and persists with **shared_preferences**.
- **Current lab output:** BMI and BMR shown from saved profile.
- Profile is loaded on app startup (see **App loader** below).

### 2. **Map tab**
- **Dark map:** CartoDB Dark (no API key).
- **Current location:** Green marker; stream updates position.
- **‚ÄúMy location‚Äù FAB:** Centers map on current position.
- **Start / Stop expedition** FAB: Starts and stops route recording.

### 3. **Route recording (laser trace)**
- With **Start expedition** on the map, each position update is appended to `routePoints`.
- **Polyline** in Neon Cyan (`#00F5FF`) is drawn on the map.
- **Stop expedition** clears the in-memory route (next start begins a new one).

### 4. **Bottom nav**
- **Map** ‚Üí map + expedition controls.
- **Home** ‚Üí Mission Control (step ring, diagnostics, Start Expedition).
- **Profile** ‚Üí Physical specs form and BMI/BMR.

### 5. **Persistence**
- **Profile:** weight, height, age, sex saved and restored.
- **Oath & XP:** oath accepted and XP saved and restored across restarts.

### 6. **App loader**
- Shows ‚ÄúINITIALIZING LAB...‚Äù while `loadFromStorage()` runs, then Oath or MainShell.

---

## New / updated files

| File | Purpose |
|------|--------|
| `lib/screens/profile_screen.dart` | Profile form and save. |
| `lib/screens/map_screen.dart` | Dark map, location, route polyline, expedition FAB. |
| `lib/screens/main_shell.dart` | Bottom nav and Map / Home / Profile. |
| `lib/main.dart` | App loader and MainShell. |
| `lib/state/system_commander.dart` | `routePoints`, `currentPosition`, load/save profile and oath. |
| `pubspec.yaml` | `shared_preferences`, `flutter_map`, `latlong2`, `geolocator`, `permission_handler`. |
| `PERMISSIONS.md` | Android/iOS location permission snippets. |

---

## What you do locally

1. **Install Flutter** and ensure `flutter` is on your PATH.
2. **Create platform folders** (if needed):  
   `cd path_pulse` ‚Üí `flutter create .`
3. **Add location permissions** using the snippets in `path_pulse/PERMISSIONS.md`.
4. **Run the app:**  
   `flutter pub get` ‚Üí `flutter run`  
   (device or emulator with location).

Then: accept the Oath (if first run), open **Map** and allow location, tap **Start expedition** and move to see the cyan route, open **Profile** and set/save specs, and use **Home** for the dashboard.

Short answer: **Cursor is where you create and edit the app. It doesn‚Äôt replace Flutter for building and running it.**

- **Creating the app in Cursor** = writing and editing the code in Cursor. You‚Äôre already doing that; the Path-Pulse Flutter project lives in your Cursor workspace.
- **Building/running the app** = still done by the **Flutter SDK** (e.g. `flutter run`, `flutter build`). You run those from **Cursor‚Äôs terminal** (or any terminal). So:
  - **Cursor** = editor (where you create and change code).
  - **Flutter** = tool that compiles and runs the app on device/emulator.

You don‚Äôt need a different editor; you use **Cursor to create**, and **Flutter to build/run**.

  path: c:\Users\HOME\.cursor\projects\2026 project\Path Pulse file\path-pulse-web\app.js
  contents: (function () {
  'use strict';

  const STORAGE_KEYS = {
    oath: 'pathpulse_oath',
    weight: 'pathpulse_weight',
    height: 'pathpulse_height',
    age: 'pathpulse_age',
    male: 'pathpulse_male',
    xp: 'pathpulse_xp',
  };

  const state = {
    oathAccepted: false,
    weight: 85,
    height: 1.8,
    age: 30,
    isMale: true,
    dailySteps: 7540,
    xp: 0,
    isMissionActive: false,
    routePoints: [],
    currentPosition: null,
    watchId: null,
  };

  let map = null;
  let userMarker = null;
  let routeLine = null;

  function bmi() {
    return state.weight / (state.height * state.height);
  }
  function bmr() {
    const base = 10 * state.weight + 6.25 * (state.height * 100) - 5 * state.age;
    return state.isMale ? base + 5 : base - 161;
  }
  function level() {
    return Math.floor(0.1 * Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, state.xp)) + 1);
  }
  function rank() {
    const l = level();
    if (l < 10) return 'RECRUIT';
    if (l < 25) return 'SCOUT';
    if (l < 50) return 'VANGUARD';
    if (l < 75) return 'BIO-COMMANDER';
    return 'APEX PATHFINDER';
  }
  function explorerId() {
    return 'PATHFINDER_' + (100 + (state.xp % 900)) + 'X';
  }
  function burn() {
    const base = state.dailySteps * 0.04 * 1.2;
    return Math.round(base);
  }
  function protocol() {
    return state.dailySteps > 10000 ? 'High-Carb Recovery' : 'Baseline Protein';
  }

  function loadStorage() {
    try {
      state.oathAccepted = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.oath) === '1';
      const w = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.weight);
      if (w != null) state.weight = parseFloat(w);
      const h = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.height);
      if (h != null) state.height = parseFloat(h);
      const a = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.age);
      if (a != null) state.age = parseInt(a, 10);
      const m = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.male);
      if (m != null) state.isMale = m === '1';
      const x = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.xp);
      if (x != null) state.xp = parseInt(x, 10);
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  function saveOath() {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEYS.oath, state.oathAccepted ? '1' : '0');
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEYS.xp, String(state.xp));
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  function saveProfile() {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEYS.weight, String(state.weight));
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEYS.height, String(state.height));
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEYS.age, String(state.age));
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEYS.male, state.isMale ? '1' : '0');
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  function showScreen(id) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.screen').forEach(function (el) {
      el.classList.add('hidden');
    });
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) el.classList.remove('hidden');
  }

  function setTab(tabName) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-pane').forEach(function (p) {
      p.classList.remove('active');
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn').forEach(function (b) {
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.tab === tabName);
    });
    const pane = document.getElementById('tab-' + tabName);
    if (pane) pane.classList.add('active');
    if (tabName === 'map' && map) {
      setTimeout(function () { map.invalidateSize(); }, 100);
    }
  }

  function updateHomeUI() {
    const targetSteps = 10000;
    const progress = Math.min(1, state.dailySteps / targetSteps);
    document.getElementById('ring-fill').style.transform = 'rotate(-90deg) rotate(' + (progress * 360) + 'deg)';
    document.getElementById('steps').textContent = state.dailySteps;
    document.getElementById('explorer-id').textContent = explorerId();
    document.getElementById('level').textContent = level();
    document.getElementById('rank').textContent = rank();
    document.getElementById('val-bmi').textContent = bmi().toFixed(1);
    document.getElementById('val-bmr').textContent = Math.round(bmr()) + ' kcal/day';
    document.getElementById('val-burn').textContent = burn() + ' KCAL';
    document.getElementById('val-protocol').textContent = protocol();

    const missionBtn = document.getElementById('btn-mission-home');
    missionBtn.classList.toggle('active', state.isMissionActive);
    document.getElementById('mission-icon').textContent = state.isMissionActive ? '‚óâ' : '‚ñ∂';
    document.getElementById('mission-label').textContent = state.isMissionActive ? 'MISSION ACTIVE' : 'START EXPEDITION';
  }

  function updateProfileUI() {
    document.getElementById('input-weight').value = state.weight;
    document.getElementById('input-height').value = state.height;
    document.getElementById('input-age').value = state.age;
    document.getElementById('sex-male').classList.toggle('active', state.isMale);
    document.getElementById('sex-female').classList.toggle('active', !state.isMale);
    document.getElementById('profile-bmi').textContent = bmi().toFixed(1);
    document.getElementById('profile-bmr').textContent = Math.round(bmr()) + ' kcal/day';
  }

  function updateExpeditionButton() {
    const btn = document.getElementById('btn-expedition');
    btn.classList.toggle('expedition-active', state.isMissionActive);
    document.getElementById('expedition-icon').textContent = state.isMissionActive ? '‚ñ†' : '‚ñ∂';
    document.getElementById('expedition-label').textContent = state.isMissionActive ? 'STOP EXPEDITION' : 'START EXPEDITION';
  }

  function initMap() {
    const center = state.currentPosition
      ? [state.currentPosition.lat, state.currentPosition.lng]
      : [51.5, -0.09];
    map = L.map('map', { zoomControl: false }).setView(center, 15);
    L.control.zoom({ position: 'topright' }).addTo(map);
    L.tileLayer('https://{s}.basemaps.cartocdn.com/dark_all/{z}/{x}/{y}{r}.png', {
      subdomains: 'abcd',
      maxZoom: 19,
    }).addTo(map);

    if (state.currentPosition) {
      userMarker = L.marker([state.currentPosition.lat, state.currentPosition.lng], {
        icon: L.divIcon({
          className: 'user-marker',
          html: '<span style="color:#39FF14;font-size:24px">‚óè</span>',
          iconSize: [24, 24],
        }),
      }).addTo(map);
    }

    routeLine = L.polyline([], { color: '#00F5FF', weight: 5 }).addTo(map);
  }

  function updateMapPosition(lat, lng) {
    state.currentPosition = { lat: lat, lng: lng };
    if (!map) return;
    if (!userMarker) {
      userMarker = L.marker([lat, lng], {
        icon: L.divIcon({
          className: 'user-marker',
          html: '<span style="color:#39FF14;font-size:24px">‚óè</span>',
          iconSize: [24, 24],
        }),
      }).addTo(map);
    }
    userMarker.setLatLng([lat, lng]);
    if (state.routePoints.length === 1) map.setView([lat, lng], 16);
  }

  function updateRouteLine() {
    if (!routeLine) return;
    const pts = state.routePoints.map(function (p) { return [p.lat, p.lng]; });
    routeLine.setLatLngs(pts);
  }

  function startWatching() {
    if (state.watchId != null) return;
    state.watchId = navigator.geolocation.watchPosition(
      function (pos) {
        const lat = pos.coords.latitude;
        const lng = pos.coords.longitude;
        updateMapPosition(lat, lng);
        if (state.isMissionActive) {
          state.routePoints.push({ lat: lat, lng: lng });
          updateRouteLine();
          state.dailySteps += Math.round(Math.random() * 4 + 8);
          updateHomeUI();
        }
      },
      function () {},
      { enableHighAccuracy: true, maximumAge: 5000 }
    );
  }

  function stopWatching() {
    if (state.watchId != null) {
      navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(state.watchId);
      state.watchId = null;
    }
  }

  function toggleExpedition() {
    state.isMissionActive = !state.isMissionActive;
    if (state.isMissionActive) {
      state.routePoints = state.currentPosition
        ? [{ lat: state.currentPosition.lat, lng: state.currentPosition.lng }]
        : [];
      updateRouteLine();
      state.xp += 10;
      saveOath();
    } else {
      state.routePoints = [];
      updateRouteLine();
    }
    updateExpeditionButton();
    updateHomeUI();
  }

  function init() {
    loadStorage();

    document.getElementById('accept-oath').addEventListener('click', function () {
      state.oathAccepted = true;
      state.xp = 0;
      saveOath();
      showScreen('main-shell');
      setTab('home');
      initMap();
      navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        function (pos) {
          updateMapPosition(pos.coords.latitude, pos.coords.longitude);
          startWatching();
        },
        function () { startWatching(); },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true }
      );
      updateHomeUI();
      updateProfileUI();
    });

    document.getElementById('abort-oath').addEventListener('click', function () {
      document.getElementById('oath-screen').classList.add('hidden');
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn').forEach(function (btn) {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
        setTab(btn.dataset.tab);
      });
    });

    document.getElementById('btn-mission-home').addEventListener('click', toggleExpedition);
    document.getElementById('btn-expedition').addEventListener('click', toggleExpedition);

    document.getElementById('btn-location').addEventListener('click', function () {
      if (!state.currentPosition || !map) return;
      map.setView([state.currentPosition.lat, state.currentPosition.lng], 16);
    });

    document.getElementById('save-profile').addEventListener('click', function () {
      const w = parseFloat(document.getElementById('input-weight').value);
      const h = parseFloat(document.getElementById('input-height').value);
      const a = parseInt(document.getElementById('input-age').value, 10);
      if (!isNaN(w) && w > 0) state.weight = w;
      if (!isNaN(h) && h > 0) state.height = h;
      if (!isNaN(a) && a > 0) state.age = a;
      saveProfile();
      updateHomeUI();
      updateProfileUI();
      alert('Baseline saved. Lab recalculated.');
    });

    document.getElementById('sex-male').addEventListener('click', function () {
      state.isMale = true;
      document.getElementById('sex-male').classList.add('active');
      document.getElementById('sex-female').classList.remove('active');
      updateProfileUI();
    });
    document.getElementById('sex-female').addEventListener('click', function () {
      state.isMale = false;
      document.getElementById('sex-female').classList.add('active');
      document.getElementById('sex-male').classList.remove('active');
      updateProfileUI();
    });

    if (state.oathAccepted) {
      document.getElementById('loader').classList.add('hidden');
      showScreen('main-shell');
      setTab('home');
      initMap();
      navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        function (pos) {
          updateMapPosition(pos.coords.latitude, pos.coords.longitude);
          startWatching();
        },
        function () { startWatching(); },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true }
      );
      updateHomeUI();
      updateProfileUI();
      updateExpeditionButton();
    } else {
      document.getElementById('loader').classList.add('hidden');
      showScreen('oath-screen');
    }
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
  } else {
    init();
  }
})();

Run Path-Pulse in your **browser** ‚Äî no Flutter or mobile SDK required.

## How to open

1. **From Cursor:** Right-click `index.html` ‚Üí **Open with Live Server** (if you have the Live Server extension), or open the file in your browser (File ‚Üí Open).
2. **From Explorer:** Double-click `index.html` or drag it into Chrome/Edge/Firefox.

**Tip:** For **location** (map and expedition) to work, use **HTTPS** or **localhost**. Opening `file:///...` may block geolocation. Easiest: use the **Live Server** extension in Cursor/VS Code so the app runs at `http://127.0.0.1:5500` (or similar).

## What‚Äôs in it

- **Oath** ‚Äî Accept the Explorer‚Äôs Oath to enter the app.
- **Home** ‚Äî Kinetic step ring, BMI/BMR, metabolic burn, Start Expedition.
- **Map** ‚Äî Dark map (CartoDB), your location, **Start/Stop Expedition** to record a route (cyan line).
- **Profile** ‚Äî Weight, height, age, sex; save baseline. BMI/BMR update from your inputs.

Data is stored in your browser (localStorage). No server or install needed.

## Folder

```
path-pulse-web/
  index.html   ‚Äî structure and tabs
  styles.css   ‚Äî Obsidian theme and layout
  app.js       ‚Äî state, map, geolocation, route, persistence
  README.md    ‚Äî this file
```

---

## Path-Pulse Web (no Flutter)

A **browser-only** version of Path-Pulse is in the **`path-pulse-web`** folder. No Flutter (or any mobile SDK) is required.

### How to run it

1. **From Cursor**
   - In the file tree, go to **Path Pulse file ‚Üí path-pulse-web**.
   - Right‚Äëclick **`index.html`** ‚Üí **Open with Live Server** (if you use the Live Server extension),  
     **or**
   - Right‚Äëclick **`index.html`** ‚Üí **Reveal in File Explorer** ‚Üí double‚Äëclick `index.html` to open it in your browser.

2. **Location (map & expedition)**  
   Browsers often block geolocation on `file://` URLs. For the map and ‚ÄúStart expedition‚Äù to work:
   - Use **Live Server** in Cursor so the app is served at something like `http://127.0.0.1:5500`,  
   **or**
   - In Chrome, when the page asks for location, allow it (and use a served URL if needed).

### What‚Äôs in the web app

| Feature | Description |
|--------|--------------|
| **Oath** | First screen; accept to enter the app. |
| **Home** | Step ring, LEVEL/RANK, BMI, BMR, metabolic burn, **Start expedition** button. |
| **Map** | Dark map (CartoDB), your location (green dot), **Start / Stop expedition** to record a cyan route. |
| **Profile** | Weight, height, age, sex; **Save baseline**; live BMI/BMR. |
| **Persistence** | Profile and oath/XP saved in the browser (localStorage). |

### Files

- **`path-pulse-web/index.html`** ‚Äî Layout and tabs (Oath, Map, Home, Profile).
- **`path-pulse-web/styles.css`** ‚Äî Obsidian theme (dark, cyan, lime).
- **`path-pulse-web/app.js`** ‚Äî Logic: state, map (Leaflet), geolocation, route recording, localStorage.
- **`path-pulse-web/README.md`** ‚Äî Short instructions (open in browser, use Live Server for location).

You can use **Cursor only** to edit and run this: open `index.html` with Live Server or in a browser. No Flutter install needed.

  path: c:\Users\HOME\.cursor\projects\2026 project\Path Pulse file\path-pulse-web\app.js
  old_string:   function loadStorage() {
    try {
      state.oathAccepted = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.oath) === '1';
      const w = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.weight);
      if (w != null) state.weight = parseFloat(w);
      const h = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.height);
      if (h != null) state.height = parseFloat(h);
      const a = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.age);
      if (a != null) state.age = parseInt(a, 10);
      const m = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.male);
      if (m != null) state.isMale = m === '1';
      const x = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.xp);
      if (x != null) state.xp = parseInt(x, 10);
    } catch (e) {}
  }
  new_string:   function haversineKm(a, b) {
    const R = 6371;
    const dLat = (b.lat - a.lat) * Math.PI / 180;
    const dLon = (b.lng - a.lng) * Math.PI / 180;
    const x = Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
      Math.cos(a.lat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(b.lat * Math.PI / 180) *
      Math.sin(dLon / 2) * Math.sin(dLon / 2);
    return R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(x), Math.sqrt(1 - x));
  }

  function routeDistanceKm() {
    if (state.routePoints.length < 2) return 0;
    let km = 0;
    for (let i = 1; i < state.routePoints.length; i++) {
      km += haversineKm(state.routePoints[i - 1], state.routePoints[i]);
    }
    return Math.round(km * 100) / 100;
  }

  function stepsFromDistanceKm(km) {
    return Math.round(km * 1300);
  }

  function getTodayKey() {
    const d = new Date();
    return d.getFullYear() + '-' + String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  }

  function getWeekStart() {
    const d = new Date();
    const day = d.getDay();
    const diff = d.getDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1);
    const mon = new Date(d);
    mon.setDate(diff);
    return mon.getFullYear() + '-' + String(mon.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(mon.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  }

  function loadHistory() {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.history);
      return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : [];
    } catch (e) { return []; }
  }

  function saveHistory(history) {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEYS.history, JSON.stringify(history));
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  function logToday(distanceKm, addedSteps) {
    const key = getTodayKey();
    const hist = loadHistory();
    let found = hist.find(function (e) { return e.date === key; });
    if (found) {
      found.distanceKm = (found.distanceKm || 0) + distanceKm;
      found.steps = (found.steps || 0) + addedSteps;
    } else {
      hist.push({ date: key, distanceKm: distanceKm, steps: state.dailySteps });
    }
    saveHistory(hist);
  }

  function getWeekStats() {
    const weekStart = getWeekStart();
    const hist = loadHistory();
    let totalKm = 0;
    let totalSteps = 0;
    hist.forEach(function (e) {
      if (e.date >= weekStart) {
        totalKm += e.distanceKm || 0;
        totalSteps += e.steps || 0;
      }
    });
    return { totalKm: totalKm, totalSteps: totalSteps };
  }

  function loadStorage() {
    try {
      state.oathAccepted = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.oath) === '1';
      const w = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.weight);
      if (w != null) state.weight = parseFloat(w);
      const h = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.height);
      if (h != null) state.height = parseFloat(h);
      const a = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.age);
      if (a != null) state.age = parseInt(a, 10);
      const m = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.male);
      if (m != null) state.isMale = m === '1';
      const x = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.xp);
      if (x != null) state.xp = parseInt(x, 10);
      const steps = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.dailySteps);
      if (steps != null) state.dailySteps = parseInt(steps, 10);
      const week = getWeekStart();
      state.missionCompletedThisWeek = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEYS.missionComplete) === week;
      var weekStats = getWeekStats();
      state.weekDistanceKm = weekStats.totalKm;
    } catch (e) {}
  }

Summary of what was added to the **web app**:

---

## New features

### 1. **Route distance & steps from expedition**
- When you **Stop expedition**, the app:
  - Computes **route distance** (km) using the Haversine formula.
  - Estimates **steps** from distance (~1,300 steps/km) and adds them to **Kinetic steps**.
- **Last route** is shown on Home (e.g. ‚ÄúLast route: 0.85 km‚Äù) after you finish an expedition.

### 2. **Weekly diagnostic ‚Äî Report tab**
- New **Report** tab in the bottom nav (between Home and Profile).
- Shows:
  - **Distance this week** (sum of all expedition distances since Monday).
  - **Today‚Äôs steps** (current step count).
  - **Verdict:** OPTIMAL EVOLUTION (‚â•2 km), STABLE PROGRESS (>0 km), or INITIATE EXPEDITION (0 km).

### 3. **Expedition mission: ‚ÄúWalk 2 km this week‚Äù**
- On **Home**, a mission card shows:
  - Progress bar for **this week‚Äôs distance** toward 2 km.
  - Text like ‚Äú0 / 2 km‚Äù (or ‚Äú2.1 / 2 km ‚úì‚Äù when done).
- When your **weekly total** reaches **2 km**, you get **+50 XP** and a checkmark; the mission is marked complete for the current week (resets next Monday).

### 4. **Persistence**
- **Daily steps** are saved so they persist across refreshes.
- **History** (date, distance, steps) is stored for the weekly total and report.
- **Mission completed** for the current week is stored so the ‚úì and bonus stay until the next week.

---

## How to try it

1. Run the app (e.g. `python -m http.server 8080` in `path-pulse-web`).
2. Open **Map** ‚Üí **Start expedition** ‚Üí move a bit ‚Üí **Stop expedition**.
3. On **Home** you should see ‚ÄúLast route: X.XX km‚Äù and the mission progress bar updated.
4. Open **Report** to see the weekly diagnostic and verdict.

The bottom nav is now: **Map | Home | Report | Profile**.

---

## QR code page

**File:** `path-pulse-web/qr.html`

**What it does:**  
When you open it in the browser **on your PC**, it shows a QR code for the app URL (e.g. `http://192.168.1.144:8080/index.html`) and the same URL as text.

---

## How to use it on your Tab 9

1. **On your PC**
   - Start the server from `path-pulse-web`:
     ```text
     python -m http.server 8080
     ```
   - In the browser, open:
     - **http://localhost:8080/qr.html**  
     or, from another device on the same Wi‚ÄëFi:
     - **http://192.168.1.144:8080/qr.html**  
     (use your PC‚Äôs IP if it‚Äôs different)

2. **On your Tab 9**
   - Open the **Camera** app (or any app that can scan QR codes).
   - Scan the QR code shown on the PC screen.
   - When it suggests opening the link, tap it.  
   The Tab 9 should open Path-Pulse at `http://YOUR_PC_IP:8080/index.html`.

3. **Same Wi‚ÄëFi**
   - Your Tab 9 must be on the **same Wi‚ÄëFi** as the PC so `http://...:8080` works.

---

**If you prefer typing:**  
The page also shows the URL under the QR code. You can type that URL into the browser on your Tab 9 instead of scanning.

  function updateFuelUI() {
    var bmrEl = document.getElementById('fuel-bmr');
    var burnEl = document.getElementById('fuel-burn');
    var balanceEl = document.getElementById('fuel-balance');
    var inputEl = document.getElementById('input-calories');
    if (bmrEl) bmrEl.textContent = Math.round(bmr()) + ' kcal';
    if (burnEl) burnEl.textContent = burn() + ' kcal';
    if (inputEl) inputEl.value = state.calorieIntake || '';
    var totalBurn = Math.round(bmr()) + burn();
    var intake = state.calorieIntake || 0;
    var balance = totalBurn - intake;
    if (balanceEl) {
      balanceEl.textContent = (balance >= 0 ? '+' : '') + balance + ' kcal';
      balanceEl.classList.toggle('surplus', balance < 0);
      balanceEl.classList.toggle('deficit', balance >= 0);
    }
  }

  function updateMapDistanceUI() {
    var hud = document.getElementById('map-distance-hud');
    if (!hud) return;
    var labelEl = document.getElementById('map-distance-label');
    var kmEl = document.getElementById('map-distance-km');
    if (state.isMissionActive) {
      var km = routeDistanceKm();
      hud.classList.remove('hidden');
      if (labelEl) labelEl.textContent = 'LIVE';

      hud.classList.remove('hidden');
      if (labelEl) labelEl.textContent = 'Last';
      if (kmEl) kmEl.textContent = state.lastRouteKm.toFixed(2);
    } else {
      hud.classList.add('hidden');
    }
  }
